<username>David Yaroshevsky< /username>< user_id>
103093163168603204128< /user_id>
<pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN0L6agdtJqtT7dyT9rDv4h30fSmAyUw6CKTDfV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures><resp>None<//resp><Text>I purchased PurCBD+ Oil from Innovet online, and had a really smooth and efficient purchasing and fulfillment experience! My product was shipped quickly and securely, and I've been extremely pleased with the quality of their products and the research they've put into their offerings. Below, I've included my review for specifically the product I purchased.

My dog, Ava, is a four-year-old border collie lab mix, and she suffers from separation anxiety and noise aversion. I rescued her two years ago, and have been working on different treatment options with her ever since, from relaxation training (a behavioral approach) to psychiatric drugs. Some methods have helped more than others, but to this day she still struggles with her main triggers and I couldn't change her relationship with them while she was on psychiatric drugs. She was able to handle her triggers perfectly until she was weaned off the drugs, at which point her behavior seemed to revert to what it was before she started taking them!

Unlike psychoactive substances, the CBD oil seems to dull her perception of her triggers, rather than dulling her response the way many psychiatric drugs do (I think this allows her to experience and adapt her own response, rather than just having an artificially altered response). It's been about a month since she started taking the oil twice daily, and I never noticed any side effects whatsoever, plus she's been handling her triggers much better than ever before! I hope one day, many months down the road, I'll be able to wean her off of the oil and see a changed relationship with her triggers, but until then I'm so pleased with the visible improvement in her quality of life with the oil as a regular supplement!</Text>< date>

< Text>
Love their breakfast plate, which comes with scramble eggs (you should ask for Salvadoran style which comes with veggies) refried beans, fried plantains and hand made tortillas, and you can get it at any time day or night. I also like their fried corn tamale. Their pupusas are ok and I usually order cheese with zucchini. I come here from time to time cause they close until 11pm which is rear for a Salvadoran restaurant to close that late. The place is at times way too loud cause their music takes over the whole place and to have a conversation you need to be louder than usual. Also the place is not as dirty but their bathroom I will use only for emergencies. The area is parking meter only, but since I usually go in the night is free.</Text>

Awesome place to take your kids, it's free until their 10 months old then it's $9 a visit or you can do a monthly plan and it's about 15 to 20 dollars a month. If you have a lot of kids it can get expensive but it's well worth it. The facilities are very clean and have toys for all ages. It is a bit small and can get busy on certain days but over all it's well worth it to allow the kids to interact with each other. It's not a daycare for anyone who wants to. know, adults go in with kids and play with them.</Review>

Fresh roast is super close to my work. Always been wanting to stop by for their famous egg waffles and coffee. I was the first customer this morning at 8 am! Lol. Uncle Jimmy welcomed me and took my order. I ordered the Pandan Egg waffles with mochi. You do have the option to add mochi or without it. < review>
Fresh Roast is a small quirky vietnamese french corner coffee shop off E. Broadway and San Gabriel Blvd on SGValley. They offer house-roasted coffee, sandwiches, smoothies, juices, HK style egg waffles, chicken wings and noodle soup. Indoor and outdoor seats were spacious, organized and well lit. Indoor vibe is welcoming and relaxing. Interior decor is filled with books, toys, memorabilia, old car plates, assorted old souvenir collections, wooden bird clocks, etc. We came here on a lazy Sunday morning breakfast. We ordered their fresh baked Croissant (ham with lettuce, egg, avocado and tomatoes) sandwich, eggwaffle and coffee. Coffee blend was  average taste. Croissant sandwich and eggwaffle was soft, tasty and fresh. Service was moderately fast. Staff were nice, competent and professional. Prices were reasonable and competitive. Free Wi-Fi (pwd required) available. Ample of street parking and back rear parking lot available.  Overall we had a good dining experience and breakfast meal. We recommend this coffee shop.</review>

< Text>
I'm just gonna call this a 5 stars night, because all the new places that I visited on this Friday Night are all going to get 5 stars from me. Heading into Fresh Roast, I was overcome with hospitality, friendly service, and satisfying coffee.

A small family-run coffee shop like this one might not be for everyone, but I suggest trying Fresh Roast at least once to experience a place that cares about their customers and coffee made with gusto. This place was supposed to be closing, but when I popped my head in to ask, I received a friendly "Of course, open for you!"

-=- Coffee Lover -=- This was the recommended coffee to get. It was sweet and had a light caramel flavor. It was not too caramel-y or too anything for that matter. It was like a smooth blend of all the sweet coffees.

-=- Waffle Bites -=- We didn't even order this, but the owner came by and said that we should try it. So awesome and so friendly. They were on the plain side, but that's what I like. These go down pretty light, so it could get dangerous if you are trying to avoid eating too much.<//Text>

< Review>
We found Fresh Roast on Yelp. The picture of the HK waffle lured us in. We love the HK waffles. You can get plain waffle, or with fillings. We tried blueberry, chocolate and mochi. Chocolate is everyone's favorite. They also serve good coffee. The friendly owner recommended #1 Coffee Lover. It's made with espresso, milk, caramel and condense milk. Just the right amount of sweetness with the bitter taste of caramel. It was great, and perfect with the waffle. It's a comfy little place where you can relax or hang out with friends.</Review>

< review>
I wasnt a big fan after trying this place. Didn't meet my expectations of HK egg waffles. I came here on a weekend because I saw yelp had some good reviews that the waffle is really good like it's from Hong Kong so I decided to give it a try since I have been craving HK waffles and haven't had it since I moved to LA. I got the durian coffee and Green tea waffle with durian and red bean. I love durian so I decided to try anything with durian. I never had durian with coffee and never came to my mind that would go together so I decided to try it and it literally just tasted like durian with coffee. Iced coffee with pieces of durian as you drink it. The green tea waffle was not the best I have tried. I probably won't be back as I had better in NY and HK so this was just okay. Didn't have the taste or texture I was looking for. There was no fluffy or puffiness that I have tasted before. I will have to continue my hunt for good hk style waffles unfortunately.<//review>

<name>Carmen Leung< /name></record></dataset><record>
<username>Toan Duong<//username>< review>
Coffee/juices/Tea/food: 4/5 stars
They roast coffee and whole sale from here so their coffee is always fresh. They have Hawaiian, blue mountain, and even luwak coffee here.  Try the siphoned coffee for kick if you haven't. The latte is on point. The house blends beans used to be better years ago with a unique flavor but now it's more like a normal flavor but still very good latte. The HK waffle is excellent. Snacks and sandwiches are very good. Noodles are just ok.

Atmosphere: 4/5 stars
If you like eclectic old country look then you'll like it here. Mom and pop kind of place. Friendly and relaxing where you can sit for awhile and forget the traffic outside.  It could use a thorough clean up and freshen up.

Service: 5/5 stars
You can get coffee/food Togo or sit in. Friendly staffs that get to know you. Mom and pop will greet you by name so service is very personal if they are not busy. They have snacks, sandwiches, and food beside coffee and more fancy coffee.

Expense: 4/5 stars
Prices are less than your local Starbucks.

Return: 6/5 stars
I've come here for decades for coffee so that's an achievement by itself.

You can see my bias in my rating do just come and support your local mom and pop coffee shop if you don't want to see a Starbucks replacing it.<//review>

<UserId.>108950671193154307598< /UserId.><Pics>None<//Pics><username>Felix Lee<//username>< Resp>
None<//Resp>
<review>For over a decade, Fresh Roast has been a popular coffee shop serving citizens of San Gabriel. It was around even before the "third-wave coffeehouse" movement began. Dating back in the late 90's and early 2000's, customers around the neighborhood came to surf the Internet at computer stations in exchange for purchasing a cup of coffee. This practice remains the same today, except customers are bringing in their own electronics, and they understand and appreciate artisan coffee much more.

Fresh Roast is one of the rare places in the San Gabriel Valley that uses a siphon to brew coffee. The siphon technique involves brewing coffee at a constant temperature, which ensures the extraction time is controlled. It yields one of the cleanest and most crisp cup of filtered coffee. Pair it with the latest roast and you have the best tasting 20oz (~2 to 3 cups) of coffee in San Gabriel.

A wide variety of single-origin coffee beans is roasted in-house by owner Jimmy. The beans are country specific, but are not sourced from specific microlots or farms like third-wave coffeeshops do. However, the beans are inexpensive at around $10 to $12 per pound except for the special Jamaican Blue Mountain Wallensford Estate ($50/lb). Third-wave coffee shops typically charge much more, in excess of $20 per pound. Jimmy seems to roast the beans a little darker than I prefer.<//review>< Date>
1450756601958< /Date>

<Date>1516508945937< /Date><Rating>1<//Rating>< Review>
Made a reservation for 9. Myself my three kids, parents and their three foster kids. Manager was great took our name over the phone and had us seated promptly. Not that it should matter but we are Hispanic. Our server was Jennifer. After our breakfast my father got up to pay the bill. We stayed at the table waiting for her to bring a box. The entrance was getting full of people waiting to be seated. We are not rude and did not push our way out. We waited until there was a clear path to the door. As we were about to leave. Jennifer our server outstreached her arms and said "Wait a minute who's paying here?" Asking the kids first then myself. I was appalled she assumed we would not pay our measly $75 bill having kids with us. I told her my Father paid. She didn't believe me and asked my Father herself. She didn't believe him either, asked "You did, you paid with a credit card?" She didn't even apologize. She made presumptions because we are Hispanic and a large party that we would be capable of skipping out on the bill. We have never been accused like that anywhere. The kids were saddened that this waitress felt the need to block us from the door. Today happens to be one of my Foster sisters birthday. Way to go Jennifer! Way to ruin what was a pleasant family breakfast. You need to get your racial profiling in check Ma'am. Needless to say we won't be visiting this IHOP anymore.<//Review>
